mandelbulb 3d parameters list
« on: February 23, 2011, 08:46:24 PM »
Reply with quoteQuote
here are some m3d parameters from around the web. 

The best idea to find find pics and websites of parameters is type in the parameter code: "mandelbulb3dv16{" and "mandelbulb3dv17{" into search boxes in Google images, Deviant art, Google text search, Bing etc... Then go to the page of any image and you will have it's parameters.
http://images.google.com/images?q=mandelbulb3dv17  (2000+ parameters with preview pics!)
http://browse.deviantart.com/?qh=&section=&q=mandelbulb3dv17 (from deviant art)
goo.gl/bPF2V (parameters of v16)
http://www.bing.com/images/search?q=mandelbulb3dv17&go=&qs=n&form=QBLH&filt=all&pq=mandelbulb3dv17&sc=0-10&sp=-1&sk= (bing images)
goo.gl/mBUwM (parameters of v17 google of deviant art)



some parameter editing tutorials by HalTenny:
http://haltenny.deviantart.com/art/Pipe-World-195354261
and fiery fire
http://fiery-fire.deviantart.com/art/Mandelbulb-3D-Negative-Tuto-195722721

Hi Evie,
Welcome to the FractalForums List.  If you can't get things to work here do a search of FractalForums for Mandelbulber 0.98. This is Buddhi's program, and it has a number of other interesting 3D fractals besides the Manbelbulb, such as Mandlelbox and KIFS fractals. Dave Makin's MMFWip3D ufm can also be downloaded from his site to make mandelbulbs. Of course there is another program out there that can also make Mandlebulbs - my 3D Fractal Raytrace program. I assume you still have Ultrafractal 5 up and running.

Somebody asked me for a "Glynn formula": there is no need to write it since the Glynn formula is simply

z = z^1.5 + c

But c is a float seed value, so this will give the requested effect. grin

EXPERIMENTAL method
« Reply #38 on: March 10, 2011, 01:12:34 PM »
Reply with quoteQuote
I am trying this method for generate "fractals". Don't know if it's pure crap... Probably ...

1. Conversion to spherical coordinates
2. Multiply angles by some factors (angles are z,y in this system, x is the distance to the origin). Multiply w too by a factor. Without this nothing will be plotted, due to DE faking (I think)
3. Revert to normal
(this is for an angular power or something like)
4. Do x=x*x - I do this with NeoSqr. Not accurate, but for preview purposes it's ok
5. Finally as usual add c

Comes out something like:

Hi Evie,
Welcome to the FractalForums List.  If you can't get things to work here do a search of FractalForums for Mandelbulber 0.98. This is Buddhi's program, and it has a number of other interesting 3D fractals besides the Manbelbulb, such as Mandlelbox and KIFS fractals. Dave Makin's MMFWip3D ufm can also be downloaded from his site to make mandelbulbs. Of course there is another program out there that can also make Mandlebulbs - my 3D Fractal Raytrace program. I assume you still have Ultrafractal 5 up and running.

A sample parameter with my newest transform _mulC3D. If cleverly used gives the triplex version of the lambda formula;

z=z*(1-z)*c

So, add a transform with constant = +1, xyz mul = -1 (does z=z*(1-z) ) and another one with cAdd-scale = +1 and all other 0 (does the required*c multiplication.) To display correctly some pretransform tricks are needed. Here the result
